Policy clarification: Spousal leave for civil union Per our updated benefits handbook, employees are eligible for up to 15 days of paid leave for the marriage or civil partnership of a domestic partner, including fiancés. We’re here to help you balance personal milestones with professional responsibilities — no judgment, just support.

Policy note: Personal Celebrations and Time Off As we approach the end of the fiscal year, please remember that employees may request leave for personal milestones such as anniversaries, birthdays, or family celebrations. These are valid reasons under our work-life balance policy, and managers are encouraged to approve them without undue delay. We understand that these moments foster long-term loyalty and emotional well-being. If you need help drafting a request, reach out to my office.

Policy clarification on personal leave for family events As per company policy, employees may apply for up to five days of personal leave for significant family milestones such as weddings, anniversaries, or birthdays. This includes ceremonial events, travel, and related logistical arrangements. Documentation is not required unless the leave exceeds three days. Please submit your request via the portal and tag it as “Family Celebration.”

Policy reminder for personal leave during peak season While we fully support employees taking time for significant life events like weddings, we must ensure coverage plans are submitted at least 14 days in advance. Last month, three managers had to scramble because wedding plans were announced the day before leave began. If your event is upcoming, please schedule a brief meeting with your supervisor to align on workload redistribution. This isn’t about inconvenience — it’s about respecting everyone’s responsibilities.
